Highways and minor ports department
Acquisition of Lands.
[G.O.(D) No. 115, Highways and Minor Ports (EAP.1),  28th April 2020,  
CˆF¬ó 15, ê£˜õK, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2051.]
No.II(2)/HWMP/266 /2020.
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-115 Cheyyur – Vandavasi – Polur Road at km 
79/400 to km 80/050 at 156. Kannanur Village, Chetpet Taluk, Tiruvannamalai District and it has already been decided 
that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed 
by the Divisional Engineer(H), Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Vandavasi after considering the cause 
shown by the owner (or) other person having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following 
notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
 Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 25087 
sq.mts of dry lands in 156. Kannanur Village, Chetpet Taluk, Tiruvannamalai District purpose of wit for Strengthening 
and widening of SH-115 Cheyyur – Vandavasi – Polur Road at km 79/400 to km 80/050.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (LA), and office of the Special 
Tahsildar (LA), Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Vandavasi in Tiruvannamalai District may be inspected 
at any time during office hours. 
Schedule
Tiruvannamalai District, Chetpet Taluk, 156. Kannanur Village

No.II(2)/HWMP/267/2020.
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of Strengthening and widening of SH-115 Cheyyur - Polur Road from KM 26/800 to KM 
28/850 at No.72.Sendivakkam Village, Maduranthakam Taluk, Chengalpattu District and it has already been decided that 
the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed 
by the Divisional Engineer(H), Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram after considering the 
cause shown by the owner (or) other person having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the 
following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
 Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 1216 


May. 13, 2020]	
Tamil  Nadu  Government  Gazette	
	
	
  227
sq.mts of Dry and Wet lands in No.72.Sendivakkam Village, Maduranthakam Taluk, Chengalpattu District for the purpose 
of Strengthening and widening of SH-115 Cheyyur - Polur Road from KM 26/800 to KM 28/850.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special District Revenue officer (Land Acquisition), Chennai-
Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram, and office of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Cheyyur Unit, may be inspected at any time during office hours.

[G.O.(D) No. 117, Highways and Minor Ports (EAP.1),  28th April 2020,

No.II(2)/HWMP/268/2020.
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be 
acquired for the Highways purpose of wit for formation of two laning extension in SH-142 Thuraiyur-Perambalur Road 
from Km.11/500 to Km.15/300 at 65.Nakkasalem Village, Alathur Taluk, Perambalur District and it has already been 
decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or 
managed by the Divisional Engineer (H), Chennai – Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Cuddalore after considering 
the cause shown by the owner (or) other person having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish 
the following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 
of 2002).
	
	
	
	
	
	
	
NOTICE
 Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 5465 
sq.mts of dry lands in 65.Nakkasalem Village, Alathur Taluk, Perambalur District for the purpose of formation of two 
laning extension in SH-142 Thuraiyur-Perambalur Road from Km.11/500 to Km. 15/300.

The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be

Palayamkottai Road from km 39/800 to km 42/600 at Seidunganallur Village, Srivaikundam Taluk, Thoothukudi District

out of the funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project,

may be do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act,

Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 7065 sq.mts 
of Manai and Wet lands in Seidunganallur Village, Srivaikundam Taluk, Thoothukudi District for the purpose of wit for

NOTICE
Under sub-Section (1) of section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34/2002), the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below and measuring an extent of 1157 Sq.m. to 
the same a little more or less needed for public purpose in order to regularize the increasing volume of Traffic and to 
maintain the free flow of vehicles, it has been proposed to widen the State Highways Road SH-63 Thanjavur–Mannargudi 
Road from km 01/850 to 02/200 km in 53.Valamirankottai Village of Thanjavur Taluk, Thanjavur District.

Corridor Project, Mannargudi and may be inspected at any time during office hours.

following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE

of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 11,163 sq.mts of 
Wet/Dry/Manai lands in Keeranur Village, Nannilam Taluk, Thiruvarur District for the purpose of width for Strengthening 
and widening of SH-23 Mayiladuthurai Thiruvarur Road from km 10/400 to 12/780 km.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kumbakonam and office of the Special Tashildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Thiruvarur, may be inspected at any time during office hours.

No.II(2)/HWMP/279 /2020.
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of Strengthening and widening of SH-142. Thuraiyur-Perambalur Road at No.66. Elanthalapatti 
Village, Alathur Taluk, Perambalur District and it has already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to 
be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Chennai 
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Salem after considering the cause shown by the owner (or) other person having 
interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 
of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 7166 sq.mts of Dry 
lands in No.66. Elanthalapatti Village, Alathur Taluk, Perambalur District for the purpose of Strengthening and widening 
of SH-142 Thuraiyur-Perambalur Road .
The plan of the lands is kept in the Office of the Special District Revenue Officer(LA), Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial 
Corridor Project, Salem and Special Tahsildar(LA), Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Perambalur may 
be inspected at any time during office hours.
Schedule
Perambalur District, Alathur Taluk, 66.Elanthalapatti Village.

[G.O.(D) No. 130, Highways and Minor Ports (EAP.1), 28th April 2020,  
CˆF¬ó 15, ê£˜õK, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2051.]
No.II(2)/HWMP/281/2020.
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be 
acquired for the Highways purpose to with for widening SH-69 Virudhachalam-Ulundurpettai Road from Km 15/445 to 
17/580 No. 26. Mangalam Ko.1 Village in Virudhachalam Taluk, Cuddalore District and it has already been decided that 
the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed 
by the Divisional Engineer(H), Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram after considering the 
cause shown by the owner or other person having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the 
following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
ofTamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 53284 sq.mts of dry 
lands in No. 26. Mangalam Ko.1 Village in Virudhachalam Taluk, Cuddalore District for purpose to with for widening 
SH-69 Virudhachalam-Ulundurpettai Road from Km 15/445 to 17/580 Km. 
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special District Revenue officer (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram and office of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project Virudhachalam may be inspected at any time during the office hours.
Schedule
Cuddalore District, Virudhachalam Taluk, 126 Mangalam Ko BLOCK-1 Village.

No.II(2)/HWMP/289/2020.
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose for widening of Widening of SH-115 Cheyyur to Polur Road from km 33/400 to 34/070 km 
in No.62 Pathiri Village in Maduranthakam Taluk, Chengalpattu District and it has already been decided that the entire 
amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the 
Divisional Engineer (H), Chennai Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Chengalpattu after considering the cause shown 
by the owner (or) other person having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice 
under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 2070 sq.mts of 
Dry lands in No,62 Pathiri Village, Maduranthakam Taluk, Chengalpattu District for the purpose of Widening of SH-115 
Cheyyur to Polur Road from km 33/400 to 34/070 km.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land Acquisition), and office 
of the Special Tashildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai-Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepruam, may be 
inspected at any time during office hours.

No.II(2)/HWMP/296/2020.
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of widening of SH-40 Tiruchendur-Ambasamudram via Palayamkottai Road from k.m 0/750 to 
54/000 k.m and 64/200 k.m to 84/900 k.m at Omanallur village, Cheranmahadevi Taluk, Tirunelveli District and it has 
already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the 
funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer (H), Chennai Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Tirunelveli 
after considering the cause shown by the owner (or) other person having interest on such lands as the case may be 
do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil 
Nadu Act 34 of 2002).

No.II(2)/HWMP/297/2020.
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of Strengthening and widening of SH-40 Tiruchendur-Ambasamudram via Palayamkottai Road 
from k.m. 0/750 to 54/000 and k.m. 64/200 k.m. to 84/900 k.m. at Ammanpuram village, Tiruchendur Taluk, Thoothukudi

NOTICE
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 4256 sq.mts of dry 
and wet lands in Ammanpuram Village, Tiruchendur Taluk, Thoothukudi District for the purpose of Strengthening and 
widening of SH-40 Tiruchendur-Ambasamudram via Palayamkottai Road from k.m. 0/750 to 54/000 and k.m. 64/200 k.m. 
to 84/900 k.m.

Industrial Corridor Project, Tirunelveli and the Office of the Special Tahsildar (L.A), Chennai Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor 
Project, Tirunelveli and may be inspected at any time during office hours.

The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule belowhave to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-191Melur-Tirupathur Road from km 10/100 to km 14/200 
at E.Malampatti (Addl) Village, Melur Taluk, Madurai District and it has already been decided that the entire amount of 
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), 
Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Tirunelveli after considering the cause shown by the owner (or) other person 
having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following noticeunder sub-section (1) of Section 15 of 
the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002). 
 
NOTICE

of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedulebelow measuring to an extent of 6597 sq.mts of Wet lands in

Tirupathur Road from km 10/100 to km 14/200.

Special Tashildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project,Tirupathur,may be inspected at any 
time during office hours.

The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below  have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of widening  of  SH-115 Cheyyur-Vandavasi-PolurRoadfromKM 65/600 to 66/600 KM at 58. 
GothandapuramVillage, Vandavasi Taluk, Tiruvannamalai District and it has already been decided that the entire amount of 
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the  Divisional Engineer(H), 
Chennai - Kanyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram after considering the cause shown by the owner (or) other 
person having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice  under sub-section (1) of 
Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34of 2002).

The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of strengthening and widening of SH-69. Virudhachalam-Ulundurpettai Road from Km 13/992 to 
15/445 inNo.26. Mangalam Ko.2Village in Virudhachalam Taluk, Cuddalore District and it has already been decided that the 
entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the 
Divisional Engineer(H), Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram after considering the cause shown 
by the owner or other person having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice under 
sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002). 
NOTICE 
 Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 42967 sq.mts of dry and wet 
lands in No. 26. Mangalam Ko.2Village in Virudhachalam Taluk, Cuddalore District for the purpose of strengthening and 
widening of SH-69. Virudhachalam-Ulundurpettai Road from Km 13/992 to 15/445 Km .  
 The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special District Revenue officer (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram and the Office of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project Virudhachalam may be inspected at any time during the office hours.Forward by rd/

No.II(2)/HWMP/313/2020. 
Officer 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule belowhave to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of strengthening and widening of SH-115 Cheyyur-Vandavasi-Polur Road from Km.81/400 to 82/920 
Km at Chetpet-IIVillage, Chetpet Taluk, Tiruvannamalai District and it has already been decided that the entire amount of 
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), 
Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Vandavasi after considering the cause shown by the owner (or) other person 
having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following noticeunder sub-section (1) of Section 15 of 
the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002). 
 
NOTICE 
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedulebelow measuring to an extent of 33645 sq.mts of dry and wet 
lands in Chetpet-II Village, Chetpet Taluk, Tiruvannamalai District for the purpose of strengthening and widening of SH-115 
Cheyyur-Vandavasi-Polur Road from Km.81/400 to 82/920 Km. 
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land Acquisition),Chennai 
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram and office of the Special Tashildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Tiruvannamalai may be inspected at any time during office hours.

Tiruvannamalai District, Chetpet Taluk, No: 155. Chetpet-II Village.

No.II(2)/HWMP/314/2020. 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below  have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-58 Chengalpattu-Kancheepuram via ArakkonamRoad 
from km 54/840 to 55/420km,Kancheepuram District and it has already been decided that the entire amount of compensation to 
be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), Chennai - 
Kanniyakumari  Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram  after considering the cause shown by the owner (or) other person 
having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice  under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of 
the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).

No.II(2)/HWMP/317/2020.. 
 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below  have to be acquired 
for the Highways for formation of Bypass in SH-95.Mohanur-Namakkal-Senthamangalam-Rasipuram Road from Km 25/085 to 
Km 26/450 in No.19. Chithambarapatti (Bypass) Village, Senthamangalam Taluk, Namakkal District and it has already been 
decided that the entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed 
by the  Divisional Engineer (H), Chennai–Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Salemafter considering the cause shown by 
the owner (or) other person having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice  under sub-
section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34of 2002). 
NOTICE 
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor of Tamil 
Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 35665 sq.mts of dryand wet lands in 
No.19. Chithambarapatti (Bypass) Village, Senthamangalam Taluk, Namakkal District for thepurpose of extension and 
strengthening of SH-95.Mohanur-Namakkal-Senthamangalam-Rasipuram  Road from Km 25/085 to Km 26/450. 
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (LAO), Chennai-Kanniyakumari 
Industrial Corridor Project, Salem and Office of the Special Tahsildar (LA), Chennai-Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, 
Perambalur may be inspected at any time during office hours.

[G.O.(D) No. 168, Highways and Minor Ports (EAP.1), 28th April 2020,  
CˆF¬ó 15, ê£˜õK, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2051.] 
No.II(2)/HWMP/319/2020. 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule belowhave to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-79 Tiruchengode-ErodeRoad from km 83/800 to 86/300 
km at30.Thokkavadi Village, Tiruchengode Taluk, Namakkal District and it has already been decided that the entire amount of 
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), 
Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Salem after considering the cause shown by the owner (or) other person 
having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following noticeunder sub-section (1) of Section 15 of 
the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002). 
NOTICE 
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 15420 sq.mts of dry lands in 
30.Thokkavadi Village, Tiruchengode Taluk, Namakkal District for the purpose of wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-79 
Tiruchengode-ErodeRoad from km 83/800 to 86/300 km. 
The plan of the lands arekept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project and office of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai Kanniyakumari 
Industrial Corridor Project, Salem,may be inspected at any time during office hours.

No.II(2)/HWMP/320/2020. 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below  have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose for widening SH-40Tiruchendur-Ambasamudram-Palayamkottai Road from Km 67/400 to 68/800 Km 
at ChokkalingapuramVillage, Cheranmahadevi Taluk, Tirunelveli District and it has already been decided that the entire amount 
of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the  Divisional Engineer(H), 
Chennai  Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Tirunelveli after considering the cause shown by the owner or other persons 
having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice  under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of 
the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil NaduAct 34of 2002). 
NOTICE 
  Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 6734 sq.mts of 
Dry/Wet lands in Chokkalingapuprami Village, Cheranmahadevi Taluk, Tirunelveli District for the purpose of Strengthening and 
widening of SH-40 Tiruchendur-Ambasamudram-Palayamkottai Road from km 67/400 to km 68/800. 
The plan of the lands is kept in the Office of the Special District Revenue Officer’s Office, Chennai Kanniyakumari 
Industrial Project, Tirunelveli and Office of the Special Tahsildar (L.A), Chennai  Kanniyakumari Industrial  Project, Tirunelveli 
and may be inspected at any time during office hours.

          The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule belowhave to be acquired for 
the Highways purpose of wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-115Cheyyur -Polur Road fromKM 18/000 to KM 20/000 at 
No.10.Perambakkam Village, Cheyyur Taluk, Chengalpattu District and it has already been decided that the entire amount of 
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), 
Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Vandhavasi after considering the cause shown by the owner (or) other 
person having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following noticeunder sub-section (1) of Section 
15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002). 
NOTICE 
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedulebelow measuring to an extent of77 sq.mts of Natham Manai 
lands in No.10.Perambakkam Village, Cheyyur Taluk, Chengalpattu District purpose of wit for Strengthening and widening of 
SH-115Cheyyur –Polur Road fromKM 18/000 to KM 20/000. 
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special District Revenue officer (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram, and office of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai  
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Cheyyur Unit, may be inspected at any time during office hours.

[G.O.(D) No. 172, Highways and Minor Ports (EAP1), 28th April 2020,  
CˆF¬ó 15, ê£˜õK, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2051,] 
No.II(2)/HWMP/323/2020. 
 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below  have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of wit for strengthening and widening of SH-115 Cheyyur-Vandavasi-Polur Road  from Km.43/825 to 
45/000 Km in No.176MaruthaduVillage, Vandavasi Taluk, Tiruvannamalai District and it has already been decided that the 
entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the 
Divisional Engineer(H), Chennai - Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Tiruvannamalai after considering the cause shown

[G.O.(D) No. 175, Highways and Minor Ports (EAP1), 28th April 2020,

No.II(2)/HWMP/326/2020. 
 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule belowhave to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-191Melur-Thirupathur Road from km 22/300 to km 
24/600 at Karuppur Village, Thirupathur Taluk, Sivagangai District and it has already been decided that the entire amount of 
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), 
Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Tirunelveli after considering the cause shown by the owner (or) other person 
having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following noticeunder sub-section (1) of Section 15 of 
the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002). 
NOTICE 
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedulebelow measuring to an extent of 25303 sq.mts of Dry and Wet 
lands in Karuppur Village, Thirupathur Taluk, Sivagangai District purpose of Strengthening and widening of SH-191Melur-
Thirupathur Road from km 22/300 to km 24/600. 
The plan of the lands arekept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land Acquisition), Tirunelveli and 
Office of the Special Tashildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Thirupathur,may be 
inspected at any time during office hours.

No.II(2)/HWMP/328/2020. 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of Strengthening and widening of SH-23 Mayiladuthurai-Thiruvarur Road from km29/613 to 30/135  
km at Magilancheri village, Nannilam Taluk, Thiruvarur District and it has already been decided that the entire amount of 
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), 
Chennai–Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kumbakonam  after considering the cause shown by the owner (or) other 
persons having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice  under sub-section (1) of 
Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002). 
 
NOTICE 
  Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule  below measuring to an extent of 3681 sq.mts of 
Wet/G.manai lands in Magilancheri Village, Nannilam Taluk, Thiruvarur District purpose of Strengthening and  widening of SH-
23 Mayiladuthurai Thiruvarur Road from km 29/613 to 30/135  km. 
The plan of the lands are  kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land Acquisition),Chennai-
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kumbakonam and office of the Special Tashildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai-
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Thiruvarur,  may be inspected at any time during office hours.

No.II(2)/HWMP/331/2020. 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of extension and strengthening of SH-142. Thuraiyur-Perambalur Roadat No.11. Kurumbalur (South) 
(Bypass) Village, Perambalur Taluk, Perambalur District and it has already been decided that the entire amount of 
compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Divisional Engineer(H), 
Chennai - Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Salem after considering the cause shown by the owner (or) other person 
having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of 
the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002). 
NOTICE 
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 20875 sq.mts of Dry lands in 
No.11.Kurumbalur (South) (Bypass) Village, Perambalur Taluk, Perambalur District for the purpose of extension and 
strengthening of SH-142 Thuraiyur-Perambalur Road from km 25/200 to 30/250 km. 
The plan of the lands is kept in the Office of the Special District Revenue Officer(LA), Chennai - Kanniyakumari 
Industrial Corridor Project, Salem and Special Tahsildar(LA), Chennai - Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Perambalur 
may be inspected at any time during office hours.

The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below  have to be acquired 
for the Highways for the purpose of extension and strengthening of SH-142.Thuraiyur-Perambalur Road from Km 25/200 to Km 
30/250 in No.11. Kurumbalur (South) Village, Perambalur Taluk, Perambalur District and it has already been decided that the 
entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the  
Divisional Engineer (H), Chennai–Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Salemafter considering the cause shown by the 
owner (or) other person having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice  under sub-
section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34of 2002). 
NOTICE 
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor of Tamil 
Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 664 sq.mts of dry lands in No.11. 
Kurumbalur (South) Village, Perambalur Taluk, Perambalur District for thepurpose of extension and strengthening of SH-
142.Thuraiyur-Perambalur Road from Km 25/200 to Km 30/250. 
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (LAO), Chennai - Kanniyakumari 
Industrial Corridor Project, Salem and Office of the Special Tahsildar (LA), Chennai-Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, 
Perambalur may be inspected at any time during office hours.

noticeunder sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).

ofTamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 372 sq.mts of Wet lands in

No.II(2)/HWMP/345/2020. 
 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of wit for Strengthening and widening of SH-58 Kancheepuram - Arakkonam Road fromKM 67/250 to 
67/700 KM at No.27 Netteri Village, Kancheepuram Taluk, Kancheepuram District and it has already been decided that the 
entire amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the 


May. 13, 2020] 
TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE 
485 
 
Divisional Engineer (H), Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram after considering the cause shown 
by the owner (or) other person having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following notice under 
sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002). 
NOTICE 
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002) the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 523 sq.mts of wet lands in 
No. 27 Netteri Village, Kancheepuram Taluk, Kancheepuram District for the purpose of widening of SH-58 Kancheepuram - 
Arakkonam Road from KM 67/250 to 67/700 KM. 
The plan of the lands is kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (LA), Chennai Kanniyakumari 
Industrial Corridor Project, Kancheepuram Special Tashildar (LA) Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, 
Kancheepuram, may be inspected at any time during office hours.

[G.O.(D) No. 195, Highways and Minor Ports (EAP.1), 28th April 2020,  
CˆF¬ó 15, ê£˜õK, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2051.] 
No.II(2)/HWMP/346/2020. 
The Governor of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be acquired 
for the Highways purpose of strengthening and widening of SH-86. Omalur – Sankakiri – Tiruchengode Roadfrom Km 12/400 to 
13/760 Km in No.86. Desavilakku (North) Village, Omalur Taluk, Salem District and it has already been decided that the entire 
amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands is to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by theDivisional 
Engineer (H), Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Salemafter considering the cause shown by the owner (or) 
other person having interest on such lands as the case may be do hereby publish the following noticeunder sub-section (1) of 
Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34of 2002). 
NOTICE 
Under Sub-Section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the land specified in the Schedule below measuring to an extent of 23755 sq.mts of dry lands in 
No.86. Desavilakku (North) Village, Omalur Taluk, Salem District for the purpose of strengthening and widening of SH-
86.Omalur – Sankakiri – Tiruchengode Roadfrom Km 12/400 to 13/760 Km. 
The plan of the lands under acquisition are kept in the office of the Special District Revenue Officer (Land Acquisition), 
Chennai Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Salem and Office of the Special Tahsildar (Land Acquisition), Chennai 
Kanniyakumari Industrial Corridor Project, Sankakiri may be inspected at any time during office hours.

  507
Home Department
(SC)
Award of the Tamil Nadu Chief Minister's Fire Service Medal for Excellence to Fire and Rescue Service  
personnel on the occasion of the Fire Service Day on 14th April 2020.
[G.O.Ms. No. 180, Home(SC), 9th April 2020, ðƒ°Q 27, Mè£K, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2051.]
	
No. II(2)/HO/347/2020—The following six Fire and Rescue Service personnel have been awarded the Tamil Nadu Chief 
Minister's Fire Service Medal for Excellence on the occasion of Fire Service Day on 14th April 2020 by the Government of 
Tamil Nadu and the recipients are eligible for the lumpsum grant at the rates noted against each:-
Sl.
No.
Name and Rank
Lumpsum grant
1.
Thiru K. Jothivel,
Station Officer,
Korukkupettai Fire & Rescue Services Station, Chennai City 
North District
Rs. 3,000/- (Rupees three thousand 
only)
2.
Thiru K. Selvan,
Leading Fireman 6764,
Tenkasi Fire & Rescue Services Station, Tenkasi District 
Rs. 2,500/- (Rupees Two thousand 
five hundred only)
3.
Thiru E. Boopalan,
Upgraded Leading Fireman 7499,
Tenkasi Fire & Rescue Services Station, Tenkasi District
Rs. 2,500/- (Rupees Two thousand 
five hundred only)
4.

Chengalpattu District.

only)
5.

District .

only)

only)
	
2.  The expenditure shall be debited to- 
"2070 - 00 - Other Administrative Service - 108 - fire Protection and Control I - State's Expenditure - AG - Chief 
Minister's Fire Service Medal for Excellence - 59 Prizes and awards". (DPC 2070 - 00 - 108 AG 5909)
Transfer of complaint on the allegations of fraudulent activities and actions detrimental to the interest of the Indian 
Red Cross Society, Tamil Nadu Branch and the Financial mismanagement to the Central Bureau of Investigation for 
investigation  under the Delhi Special Police Establishment Act.
[G.O.Ms. No. 181, Home(Pol. VII), 9th April 2020, ðƒ°Q 27, Mè£K, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2051.]
	
No. II(2)/HO/348/2020—Under Section 6 of the Delhi Special Police Establishment Act, 1946 (Central Act 25 of 
1946), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby accords his consent to the extension of the powers and jurisdiction of members 
of the Delhi Special Police Establishment in the whole of the State of Tamil Nadu to investigate on the complaint made 
by the Deputy Secretary to Governor, Office of the Hon'ble Governor, Tamil Nadu, in respect of allegations of fraudulent 
activities and actions detrimental to the interest of the Indian Red Cross Society, Tamil Nadu Branch and the financial 
mismanagement.
	
	
S.K. Prabakar,
	
	
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.
